  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<span id="freeTextContainer15468689694458741213">I used to think my sister and I were just two nice southern girls who’d get married in a few years and settle down to a quiet life.   <span id="freeText15468689694458741213" style="display:none">I used to think my sister and I were just two nice southern girls who’d get married in a few years and settle down to a quiet life. Then I discovered that Alina and I descend, not from good wholesome southern stock, but from an ancient Celtic bloodline of powerful sidhe-seers, people who can see the Fae. Not only can I see the terrifying otherworldly race, but I can sense the sacred Fae relics that hold the deadliest of their magic.<br /><br />When my sister was found dead in a trash-filled alley in Dublin, I came over to get answers. Now all I want is revenge. And after everything I’ve learned about myself, I know I have the power to get it….<br /><br />MacKayla Lane’s ordinary life underwent a complete makeover when she landed on Ireland’s shores and was plunged into a world of deadly sorcery and ancient secrets. <br /><br />In her fight to stay alive, Mac must find the Sinsar Dubh–a million-year-old book of the blackest magic imaginable, which holds the key to power over both the worlds of the Fae and of Man. Pursued by Fae assassins, surrounded by mysterious figures she knows she cannot trust, Mac finds herself torn between two deadly and irresistible men: V’lane, the insatiable Fae who can turn sensual arousal into an obsession for any woman, and the ever-inscrutable Jericho Barrons, a man as alluring as he is mysterious. <br /><br />For centuries the shadowy realm of the Fae has coexisted with that of humans. Now the walls between the two are coming down, and Mac is the only thing that stands between them.…</span>

//<![CDATA[
  var timer_314843_end_at = 308042 + new Date().getTime()/1000;

  function timer_314843_updateTimer() {
    var time_left = "";
    var secs_left = timer_314843_end_at - new Date().getTime()/1000;

    if(secs_left <= 0) {
      document.getElementById("timer_314843").innerHTML = "closed";
      clearInterval(timer_314843_updater);
      return;
    }

    var minutes_left = secs_left / 60;
    var hours_left = minutes_left / 60;
    var days_left = Math.floor(hours_left / 24);

    if(days_left > 0) {
      if(false){
        time_left += days_left + ":";
      }else{
        time_left += days_left + " days and ";
      }
    }
    if(false){
      time_left += Math.floor(hours_left%24/10)
      time_left += Math.floor(hours_left%24)%10 + ":";
    }else{
      time_left += Math.floor(hours_left%24) + ":";
    }
    time_left += Math.floor(minutes_left%60/10);
    time_left += Math.floor(minutes_left%10) + ":";
    time_left += Math.floor(secs_left%60/10);
    time_left += Math.floor(secs_left%10);

    document.getElementById("timer_314843").innerHTML = time_left;
  }

  timer_314843_updateTimer();
  var timer_314843_updater = setInterval(timer_314843_updateTimer, 100);

<div id="review_54450102" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/54450102" />
    <a title="Shannon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon"><img alt="Shannon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572638169p2/2016128.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/54450102?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shannon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shannon" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon">Shannon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=dumb-female-characters">dumb-female-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=ireland">ireland</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=color-red">color-red</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=made-me-angry">made-me-angry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=forgot-to-drink-the-kool-aid">forgot-to-drink-the-kool-aid</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=2011">2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=fairies">fairies</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer54450102" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6235888874938691849"><b>I don't like Mac. I don't like Barrons. I'm not even really enjoying the story.</b> So why keep reading, you might ask. Masochism? Some vague sense of loyalty toward friends on here who constantly berate me with, "Keep reading, it gets better!!!" Or, is it really just my obsessive compulsive NEED to see how something ends? Probably a little of all three.<br/><br/>Once we get into the meat of the story, it's very plain to see that Mac hasn't changed, although she sure would like us to think so. <b>She goes on and</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6235888874938691849" style="display:none"><b>I don't like Mac. I don't like Barrons. I'm not even really enjoying the story.</b> So why keep reading, you might ask. Masochism? Some vague sense of loyalty toward friends on here who constantly berate me with, "Keep reading, it gets better!!!" Or, is it really just my obsessive compulsive NEED to see how something ends? Probably a little of all three.<br /><br />Once we get into the meat of the story, it's very plain to see that Mac hasn't changed, although she sure would like us to think so. <b>She goes on and on about how she's isn't a dumb kid anymore and she knows more now than she did just weeks ago, but really she doesn't.</b> She still makes dumb mistakes. She still talks about her clothes and appearance. She still keeps Barrons in the dark with things she should have told him in the first place to save them both from trouble. If anything, she acts MORE arrogant and entitled in this book than the last. She's a fancy sidhe-seer now, she doesn't need to worry about some pesky humans. <br /><br />"My problems were so much bigger than this. It was an epic waste of my time."<br /><br />She says this after being interrogated about the death of a human. She wanes back and forth over wanting to save all of humanity or only caring about herself and her family. If you save the world, then you ultimately save your family. She's still very selfish and immature in this book and it's hard to take her seriously.<br /><br /><b>My main problem with Glam-girl Mac and fierce sidhe-seer Mac is the inconsistencies that pop up.</b> True, these trials she's gone through were thrusted upon her and she's dealt with them in a very short amount of time. But she constantly slides back to the Before Mac so much that you want to just slap some sense into her. Stop flirting with boys. Quit getting dressed up in nice clothes. Don't go blurting to a stranger/sidhe-seer in public that you can see the Fae too. If you want me to think you're serious about being a badass and that you've changed, (like you've told me NUMEROUS times throughout this book,) then actually SHOW me with your actions. Get serious, train, learn some basic self defense at least! <b>If your problems are as big as you think, then prepare for them.</b> Don't tell me you've changed when you haven't.<br /><br /><b>Barrons is still a dick.</b> He abuses her and she makes excuses for him. I think I know who/what he is though. I won't say though, but I have told a certain someone who shares my prediction. We'll see if we're right.<br /><br /><b>V'Lane is ... interesting.</b> I compared him to Mircea from the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/67513.Touch_the_Dark" rel="nofollow noopener">Cassie Palmer</a> series, and even though I fear being flayed alive by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/355739-the-flooze-michelle-m" rel="nofollow noopener">The Flooze,</a> he's the best comparison I can make. They're both insanely gorgeous, immortal, want a lowly human woman who has unique powers, and view humans as tools to further their goals. I find him to be the most interesting character in the whole series.<br /><br />A couple of <b>nitpicks</b> that probably won't bother many people, but did bother me:<br /><br />Spoilers for Darkfever: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Regarding the cars parked in the alley. Why leave them? Why not hire someone to come pick them up and dispose of them. Barrons has to be familiar with a chop shop or two. <b>If a bunch of people were murdered and their cars were left behind my work and/or place of residence, I would find some way to get rid of them so I couldn't be interrogated about them.</b> If the cars hadn't been there, O'Bannion's brother wouldn't have had a reason to grill Mac and be suspicious of the book store though. I hate when the plot is forced in this manner. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>The use of acronyms.</b> I can't imagine Barons saying OOP. I understand the need for acronyms, they do have their place, but it bothers me when it's constantly used in a novel. Just spell your words out! <br /><br /><b>Asking question after question after question.</b> Do we really need one or more paragraphs of just questions that Mac is thinking in her head? There has to be a better way to integrate this into the novel.<br /><br /><b>The constant spewing of metaphors.</b> People don't think or talk like that, so <i>stop it</i>.<br /><br /><b>I thought this book was weaker than the last, and I felt angrier while reading it.</b> Maybe I shouldn't have waited so long in between books and let people gently (and not so gently) prod me into reading this. Is it possible that all of the hype surrounding this series and the recent release of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7304203.Shadowfever__Fever___5_" title="Shadowfever (Fever, #5) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Shadowfever</a> has soured my experience? It's very possible. I am trying to give this series a chance, but so far it hasn't won me over.<br /><br />Here's my review of the first book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45912760" rel="nofollow noopener">Darkfever</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6235888874938691849" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy-fae-and-fairies">fantasy-fae-and-fairies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=hot-guys-alphas-rawr">hot-guys-alphas-rawr</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy-urban">fantasy-urban</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1058459533" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8381986156365557508"><b>Fifth Read - July 2020: 5 stars<br/>Fourth Read - December 2017: 5 stars!!! <br/>Third Read - October 2015: 5 stars!!!<br/>Second Read - November 2014: 4 stars<br/>First read - September 2014: 4 stars</b><br/><br/>Read it again! LOL Still love it.<br/><br/>Previous: I don't know what else I can say except that I still loved it. This is the Third Official Re-read for the MacHalo Group and I tagged along because some hadn't read it yet. So.... good enough reason for me to read it again! :))<br/><br/>I'll always be biased for this series and I love Ba</span>
  <span id="freeText8381986156365557508" style="display:none"><b>Fifth Read - July 2020: 5 stars<br>Fourth Read - December 2017: 5 stars!!! <br>Third Read - October 2015: 5 stars!!!<br>Second Read - November 2014: 4 stars<br>First read - September 2014: 4 stars</b><br><br>Read it again! LOL Still love it.<br><br>Previous: I don't know what else I can say except that I still loved it. This is the Third Official Re-read for the MacHalo Group and I tagged along because some hadn't read it yet. So.... good enough reason for me to read it again! :))<br><br>I'll always be biased for this series and I love Barrons and Mac and the world so much! This series made - and still makes - me fall in love with reading. Every time.<br><br><i>Our first annual re-read of the Fever series with the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-another-buddy-read" rel="nofollow noopener">MacHalo group</a> starts October 26, 2015! Here's the schedule (sorry, I can't keep to a schedule with this series - it takes over and I have to devour it once I start):<br><br>Darkfever: October 26<br>Bloodfever: November 9<br>Faefever: November 23<br>Dreamfever: December 7<br>Shadowfever: December 21<br>Iced: January 5<br>Burned: January 12</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428686157ra/14468071.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>New thoughts on third read:</b> Wow. How did I ever give this anything less than 5 stars?!?!?! This book is amazingly strong on world-building and we get our first glimpse of several future KEY players, like Dani, Christian, Ryodan, Rowena... I found the scenes with Barrons so much more poignant and "full of feels." KMM did some amazing writing and story-telling here. I still remain SUCH a fangirl for this series. For me, it holds up 100%.<br><br><b>Original second re-read thoughts: </b> I kept my original rating.<br><br>BARRONS. In this re-read, I found myself just waiting for the Barrons sections to come up. Never enough Barrons.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416498048i/11978886._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416498048i/11978887.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416498048i/11978888._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book introduced some great new characters and expanded some characters that were barely introduced in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112750.Darkfever__Fever___1_" title="Darkfever (Fever, #1) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Darkfever</a>. There was more world-building in this one than action. It wasn't until the last 30% of the book or so before it became a page-turner. But I still loved reading about the world KMM has created. A lot of interesting things happen in this, lots of little things, that will prove to all add up as the books go on. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I love that Barrons tattooed Mac anyway because she should have let him and he proved that he knows what he's talking about. Loved the almost-sex scene in the Burren. Y-u-m. I totally forgot the reaper/specter Mac kept seeing was Malluce! So it was like reading it for the first time. I think he made a good villain.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>Mac still clings to her old life and mindset a few times, but she learns fast. It's only been a few months and she becomes a bad-ass in this one. It's funny to read my original review because it looks like I was already having Barrons-angst because I thought he wasn't in it enough. (Mac meets and has interactions with several -some of them new- characters. Like I said above, there are a lot of conversations and inner monologues in this one.)<br><br><b>Original review:</b><br><br>Another great addition to the Fever series. I liked this one better than the first and there was a lot of action and wonderful world-building. I do hope Barrons doesn't stay the same enigmatic character for every book. He dashes in, helps Mac, they have sexually-charged banter, and he disappears again. I can already feel that would get old if it remains that way book to book.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/104298566?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tatiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tatiana" href="/user/show/2250020-tatiana">Tatiana</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

           <span class="uitext reviewText">all fans of urban fantasy</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Tatiana by: </span>
      Kat Kennedy
  </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer104298566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5102982635644807215"><b>Updated 12/10/14</b><br/>Oh, poor me, drowning in mysteries. It's still fun to read, even knowing who is what and does what why. It actually shows how well planned this whole series had been.<br/><br/>First I want to thank <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3270188' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kat</a> for recommending this series to me. So far it's been exceeding my expectations and I hope it will continue doing so. <br/><br/>In this installment MacKayla Lane continues her search for Sinsar Dubh, a powerful Unseelie artifact containing the deadliest Fae magic. She is recovering from the ordeal she </span>
  <span id="freeText5102982635644807215" style="display:none"><b>Updated 12/10/14</b><br />Oh, poor me, drowning in mysteries. It's still fun to read, even knowing who is what and does what why. It actually shows how well planned this whole series had been.<br /><br />First I want to thank <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3270188" rel="nofollow noopener">Kat</a> for recommending this series to me. So far it's been exceeding my expectations and I hope it will continue doing so. <br /><br />In this installment MacKayla Lane continues her search for Sinsar Dubh, a powerful Unseelie artifact containing the deadliest Fae magic. She is recovering from the ordeal she experienced at the end of the previous book and at the same time has to face the aftermath of her actions - Inspector O'Daffy is getting very interested in finding out more about the Dark Zone and why Mac is not going back home; Malluce's death is still uncertain; Rocky O'Bannion's brother, Derek, surfaces to poke around in Mac's business; and finally, a mysterious specter keeps following MacKayla around giving her creeps...<br /><br />In my opinion, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/344262.Bloodfever__Fever___2_" title="Bloodfever (Fever, #2) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloodfever</a> is even better than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112750.Darkfever__Fever___1_" title="Darkfever (Fever, #1) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Darkfever</a>. The Fae world is getting wider, Moning gets us deeper into the lore which is very exciting. We get to know Mac much better and I like her quite a bit. I like her humor and her upbeat personality, I enjoy seeing her grow and change and learn about her abilities. Death-by-sex Fae Prince V'lane is even more mysterious and his intentions toward Mac are unclear. Same applies to Barrons, who is a total enigma. The Mac/Jericho chemistry is off the charts! I simply LOVE these two. Jericho is slowly but surely climbing up the list of my favorite fictional hunks, but he'd better stop roughing up Mac if he ever wants to get to the top of it, because I don't care for this kind of thing. <br /><br />All in all, a great book. It doesn't have much of a resolution in terms of the main story arc (which is not a problem for me), but the minor story arc is as interesting, intense, dark and edgy. I am planning to get my hands on <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2702704.Faefever__Fever___3_" title="Faefever (Fever, #3) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Faefever</a> very soon.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5102982635644807215" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2943314344970146790">The second installment of Bloodfever is intense, powerful, dramatic and clever.<br/><br/>We see a great deal of character growth from out favorite characters as well as a progression in the plot, albeit a small one.<br/><br/>The writing is, as always, stylish and immersive. The world is complicated, mysterious and intriguing.<br/><br/>Overall, this book is a fantastic second installment in what is an amazing, refreshing and enjoyable series.<br/><br/>PS. I'm either going to kill Barrons sooner or later, or do very, very, very naughty </span>
  <span id="freeText2943314344970146790" style="display:none">The second installment of Bloodfever is intense, powerful, dramatic and clever.<br /><br />We see a great deal of character growth from out favorite characters as well as a progression in the plot, albeit a small one.<br /><br />The writing is, as always, stylish and immersive. The world is complicated, mysterious and intriguing.<br /><br />Overall, this book is a fantastic second installment in what is an amazing, refreshing and enjoyable series.<br /><br />PS. <div id="review_139400152" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/139400152" />
    <a title="Lyndsey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4224396-lyndsey"><img alt="Lyndsey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1288890060p2/4224396.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/139400152?book_show_action=true">Jan 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lyndsey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lyndsey" href="/user/show/4224396-lyndsey">Lyndsey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4224396-lyndsey?shelf=reviewed-2011">reviewed-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4224396-lyndsey?shelf=reviewed-5-stars">reviewed-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4224396-lyndsey?shelf=about-faerie-fey-folk">about-faerie-fey-folk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4224396-lyndsey?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer139400152" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2506187618026921795">Possible minor spoilers if you haven't read the first book and if any of my random ramblings turn out to be true...<br/><br/>At the beginning of the book, we join Mac just after she finds out that she was adopted. Immediately, she begins to act like her parents just dropped off the face of the earth, and she starts referring to her sister as her only real family. Her attitude instantly turned ungrateful. Yes, she was just being a drama queen, but I know for a fact that you can love someone who isn't relat</span>
  <span id="freeText2506187618026921795" style="display:none">Possible minor spoilers if you haven't read the first book and if any of my random ramblings turn out to be true...<br /><br />At the beginning of the book, we join Mac just after she finds out that she was adopted. Immediately, she begins to act like her parents just dropped off the face of the earth, and she starts referring to her sister as her only real family. Her attitude instantly turned ungrateful. Yes, she was just being a drama queen, but I know for a fact that you can love someone who isn't related to you just as much as someone who is. The fact that she is not technically related to them doesn't mean that they are no longer her family. That's really my only gripe about Mac in this book. I still think she kicks ass, just give your parents some credit! She actually had the guts to say "He was lucky I was even calling him Dad at all!" Really? At least she recanted it fairly quickly when he shows up all worried about her. After that, she seems mostly back to normal with them again.<br /><br />I'm starting to feel bad for Mac, though. I mean she's been mystically undressed and nearly performing involuntary sex acts in public (who hasn't?), rape-kissed by a drunken Irish man (uh, ditto), hit on by two seemingly normal history nerds (I persist, who hasn't?) and she's also teased inexorably, and now kissed and dry-humped, by the hot man she spends 90% of her time with (who wouldn't want to be?) yet she STILL isn't getting any.<br /><br />I'll warn you now that when i start to think about Jericho, my mind goes into a mixed state of paranoia and reckless abandon. It's no secret how I feel about Barron's name. But the way I feel in general about Jericho Zigor Barrons, or as I like to call him, J-Ziggy, is best summed up with this redonkulously articulate rant: love love loooooove adore gaaaaawd hellaluyah ahgagwhjrhfjfjkd mothreffenyes ahhhhhhhh!! !#%@?!/%#+!)$: *confetti popping out of head*<br /><br />Barrons is standoff-ish, confident and snarky, yet endlessly intriguing. He is the kind of guy who can make you feel everything and nothing at the same damn time. Not to mention, he likes to chain up women while they are wearing skimpy bikinis. Cough*jabbathehutt*Cough. Except, I probably wouldn't mind being chained up by him. Barrons, I mean, not Jabba. Obviously.<br /><br />Oh shiz! Why does Barrons have chains readily available in his basement???? For chaining up people as he feeds on them? For chaining up the Seelie? What-the-fa??? Fuuuuuudgin Fudge! He's Unseelie, isn't he?!?! It's a rhetorical question! Dang it! I don't want to know, wait, yeah I do. No. No, I don't.<br /><br />Yeah, I'm going crazy and I tried to warn you. Uh. Now I'm freaked out. Anyway, sooooo, I was thinking about who could pull off playing him in a movie. It would have to be someone very good with the eyes. Jeric-- er, Barrons uses a lot of non-verbal communication, which I find very sexy. So it would have to be someone like Ian Somerhalder AKA 'Smolder'holder. He is really very good with the "looks" but I'm not sure he could pull off the really long hair that Barrons has. And he's awfully pale, so not necessarily him. Ideas, anyone? Ah who cares, I just wanted to think about him. *sigh*<br /><br />I also have to give a big "hell yeah" to Mac for not caving to the demands of any of the several groups of people vying for her servitude. She refuses to take the easy way out and be ordered around blindly for each one's "higher" purpose. Not even with Barrons. Proudly and unbiasedly, she chooses her own higher purpose, and I have to applaud her for that. Like she herself says, she is no one's puppet, which cannot be said for many heroes or heroines in fantasy novels. Normally, someone discovers them, tells them about their abilities, teaches them to harness their powers, and then tells them exactly what to do with them. She does her best to not let that happen and chooses what she thinks is best, not what the others tell her is.<br /><br />The author's knack for introducing small amounts of information at a time, interspersed amongst the action, leads to a captivating experience. Too much information is never given up. We the readers, like Mac, have to earn the privilege of learning more about this strange world. There are no info-dumps in this series. And I appreciate it.<br /><br />In short, I loved it. And Eeeep! There's the next one sitting on my shelf!! This one ends on a bit of a cliffhanger, so I think I have to go now... Can't wait to get back to Barrons. *sigh*<br /><br />My review for the first book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/137616665" rel="nofollow noopener">Darkfever</a>. Spoiler FREE.<br /><br />For the third book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/140134045" rel="nofollow noopener">Faefever</a>. Spoiler FREE.<br /><br />The fourth book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/143396869" rel="nofollow noopener">Dreamfever</a>. Spoiler FREE.<br /><br />The fifth and final book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/144311666" rel="nofollow noopener">Shadowfever</a>. Spoiler alert!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2506187618026921795" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

It didn’t want to. It likes it there.”<br/><br/>“Far beneath me, in the marrow of the ground, something bayed.”<br/><br/>“American?”<br/>I nodded. “You?” He didn’t sound Irish.<br/>“Little of this, little of that. Nothing special.</i></span>
  <span id="freeText17548845501906873349" style="display:none"><b>WARNING: Every quote in this review is a spoiler or a mindfuck.<br /><br />UN-WARNING: If you haven’t read the entire series, you won’t understand a single one and nothing will be spoiled for you.</b><br /><br /><i>“Barrons has something the rest of us don’t have…there’s something that never crawled all the way out of the swamp. It didn’t want to. It likes it there.”<br /><br />“Far beneath me, in the marrow of the ground, something bayed.”<br /><br />“American?”<br />I nodded. “You?” He didn’t sound Irish.<br />“Little of this, little of that. Nothing special.” He smiled and winked. Dreamy eyes, long dark lashes. <br /><br />“Alina was wearing this yellow skirt and sweater set, and you were dressed from head to toe in pink, Mac, with a little rainbow ribbon tied around a blond wisp of your hair.”<br /><br />“If I was a minnow and they were sharks, he (Barrons) was one of those yet undiscovered fish that lurk in the deepest, darkest reaches of the ocean where sunlight and man never go.”<br /><br />“Never believe anything’s dead until you’ve burned it, poked around in its ashes, and then waited a day or two to see if anything rises from them.”<br /><br />“He’s dying, you know.” - Mac<br />“Good for him.” – Barrons<br /><br />“I played volleyball with my sister. We drank Coronas in the sun.”<br /><br />“…we’d paid a terrible price…it had been our greatest shame…we’d made ourselves forget.”<br /><br />“I used to have a recurring nightmare when I was a child. A dream of four distinct, subtly varied tastes…I tasted one of the vile ones now…regret.”</i><br /></span>

<div id="review_243032612" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/243032612" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/243032612?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-i-o">authors-i-o</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=favorites-books">favorites-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer243032612" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7129480341701295018">Did I ever think I would get into reading urban fantasy?? Before Fever Series….absolutely NO….and now here I am ….unable to stop reading a genre I have not had much interest….apart from the Lord of the Rings books (which blew me away!!!). <br/>I immediately started reading Bloodfever, the 2nd book of Karen Marie Moning’s Fever Series after turning the last page of the 1st book, Darkfever,which I reviewed, <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112750.Darkfever'>http://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11...</a> <br/><br/>I am back into the dark world of the Fae,….. MacKayla L</span>
  <span id="freeText7129480341701295018" style="display:none">Did I ever think I would get into reading urban fantasy?? Before Fever Series….absolutely NO….and now here I am ….unable to stop reading a genre I have not had much interest….apart from the Lord of the Rings books (which blew me away!!!). <br />I immediately started reading Bloodfever, the 2nd book of Karen Marie Moning’s Fever Series after turning the last page of the 1st book, Darkfever,which I reviewed, <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112750.Darkfever">http://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11...</a> <br /><br />I am back into the dark world of the Fae,….. MacKayla Lane has discovered and accepted and come to terms of the gift of being a sidhe seer, with special powers, one of these being the ability to sense the Sinsar Dubh, an ancient book of the blackest magic even seen, which holds the key to the balance of power between the Fae and humans. It’s the only thing that will save humanity from being destroyed by the Fae.<br /><br />I am so totally crazy about Mac. I love her view of her world…she’s lost a bit of that “I’m so into pink”…not totally at this point. She realizes that she will do anything to survive..she will bend the any rules, make alliances with anyone who can help her find her sister’s killer, fulfill Alina’s last request before she died and the answer to what her role is in this power struggle between humans and fae? <br />You can still feel her vulnerability, her insecurities but as she discovers more about herself, the stronger and more determined she becomes. When she says “What had changed was me” at the end, I realized how far she has come and how much more she will have to go through before finding all the answers. I loved Mac’s optimism…even when things look dark and scary she still tries to see a bit of “sun, pink” ahead of her. She has such an amazing way of analyzing things that are happening in her life…and wow….it’s like going on a rollercoaster ride. Non-stop action!!!!!!!!!<br /><br />She is still living at Barron’s Books &amp; Baubles..I love this bookstore…I could live there forever, surrounded by books and nothing else…no wait…I would want Jericho Barrons with me there with me!!!!!!! <br /><br />Jericho Z Barrons – I AM SO TOTALLY INTO HIM!!!!! He’s one of the most exciting heroes’ in a book, EVER…amazing, mysterious, secretive, gorgeous, sexy, stylish, rich, classy….I could go on and on…but u get the idea ……he’s beyond HOT…he’s the kind of man any woman would be dazzled, fascinated and…enthralled by!!!!!!!! This is not a romance series, has no or very few sex scenes but you can certainly feel the chemistry, the heat, the sizzle between him and Mac..of course both try to fight it and I can’t wait to see what happens between the two. Jericho is very protective over Mac but does he have an ulterior motive? What is he? A seelie, unseelie, druid, fae…how old is this guy…is he immortal ……she can feel something in him that is not totally human. Can she trust him? What does he want from her?<br /><br />And then, there’s V’lane….I keep thinking…lane, lane…is there any connection or meaning to Mac’s family name Lane???? The Seelie Prince who also wants something from her…but is he really who he says he is???? What does he want from Mac? She knows he is not telling her everything but she decides to forge an alliance with him as well…which drives Jericho crazy of course!!!!! In the growing darkness, V’lane is the one who takes her to the Faery world …..where she spends time in the sun…..loved the scene on the beach in Cancun…really funny….and when Mac spends time with her sister…that was so poignant.<br /><br />Mac discovers she is not the only sidhe seer and tries to link up with them but their Mistress, Rowena, who Mac first met in Darkfever, is not prepared to have her join the group unless she agrees to obey her..which of course Mac is so just not going to do!!!!!!!! What give up her spear??? Rowena is such a wicked character…I so hate her and hope she comes to a really gruesome ending!!!!!!!! <br /><br />Her characters are so vivid, so real, so believable. Fast story pacing made me at times so breathless like I had was running a marathon!!!!! <br />Dani, the teenage sidhe seer with her sword and “speed”, Malluce…we discover what happens to this vampire…and what evil he does to Mac…shiver……the Lord Master, who Mac still believes killer her sister (imo…he didn’t) but he’s definitely dark….and evil…I mean bringing the evil and ugly unseelie into the human world…. Christian…loved how the author brings in a bit from her Highlander Series….<br /><br />The more we learn about Mac’s world, the more questions come up. You think you know something…and then…wam…so totally different to what you thought!!!!!!!<br /><br />This is such a compelling series…I just can’t get enough. Non-stop reading……Can’t wait to start book 3 next. Karen Marie Moning is an incredible writer and I can’t get enough of her stories.<br /><br />I liked the Glossary at the back of the book…explains Mac’s World and also you get to know how to pronounce all those Celtic words!!!!!!!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7129480341701295018" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2362307568" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2362307568" />
    <a title="Princess under cover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9604542-princess-under-cover"><img alt="Princess under cover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541254101p2/9604542.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2362307568?book_show_action=true">May 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Princess under cover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Princess under cover" href="/user/show/9604542-princess-under-cover">Princess under cover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2362307568" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3868408296278929429">I am speechless. Where do I begin?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495140549ra/22790249.gif' width='500' height='225' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It was sort of good, I was even heading toward 4 stars when I started the book, giving me interesting, emotionally connective banter (see my notes) that I was starting to feel glad I continued with Book 2. But right now, unless my reading buddy group dragged me or persuaded me with arguments too powerful to resist, I am NOT getting Book 3 or any other book in the series. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517855316ra/25008206.gif' width='245' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Where to begin with the disappointment? I will preface by saying that maybe my expectations </span>
  <span id="freeText3868408296278929429" style="display:none">I am speechless. Where do I begin?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495140549ra/22790249.gif" width="500" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was sort of good, I was even heading toward 4 stars when I started the book, giving me interesting, emotionally connective banter (see my notes) that I was starting to feel glad I continued with Book 2. But right now, unless my reading buddy group dragged me or persuaded me with arguments too powerful to resist, I am NOT getting Book 3 or any other book in the series. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1517855316ra/25008206.gif" width="245" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Where to begin with the disappointment? I will preface by saying that maybe my expectations about the book/ series is just wrong. And if so, I feel kind of bad about giving a low rating because of my own misaligned expectations. Nevertheless, I paid for the books and read them. So the low rating stands.<br><br><b>My review of Book 1 is still how I feel about Book 2. With the following adds:</b><br><br>* Events that happen in this series seem to be planned so that the reader can slowly discover the various powers of the various characters, and the ultimate mystery that keeps people going - who is Jericho Barrons? What does he want with the book? What do the other characters want with the book? (but the other characters are secondary.) <b>The most compelling character in this series for me is not the heroine, I honestly couldn't care less for her. The only compelling character is JB.</b> And if I'm in a better mood I might pick up Book 3 just to see where JB is headed. OR, I might just read other people's reviews and save myself the $ and time.<br><br>* Given above, <b>events in this series don't seem to follow much plot or evolution. They're just devices to pepper in more mystery and pseudo discovery</b> - Oh, Malluce isn't really who we thought. He's just weirder and scarier. And the twenty odd pages of torture was for... what purpose exactly?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1525199580ra/25465762.gif" width="500" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>* There's no real emotional connection between the characters.</b> I said this already for Book 1 and I was hoping things would change in Book 2 and was almost optimistic they would, and then we're back to flatness. There's a pseudo sex scene that is extremely weird and displaced given the situation and did nothing to further the relationship between the two main characters. I am left deeply unsatisfied after reading it.<br><br>I don't get it. Is this a paranormal thriller? paranormal horror book? certainly not a paranormal romance, nor really all that fantasy like. But maybe I haven't read enough fantasy books to judge. It's just weird.<br><br>I'm stumped.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1525199580ra/25465761.gif" width="480" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="3868408296278929429" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans">✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6283277-bloodfever">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=br-2015">br-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=br-2014">br-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=black-listed-author">black-listed-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=2015">2015</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1104545868" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5847993867159585632"><b>First reread with my girl <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31718503-tanya' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tanya</a>, January 2015.<br/><br/>Original rating: 4<br/>New rating: 3.5</b><br/><br/><b>You know how this is going to go right?</b> My first review for this book was written just two months ago so don't you expect me to write another one so soon. <b>Hey, I have a life outside of GR you know (well, more or less)</b>. All you'll be getting from me is another episode in the <b>Fever Freak's Facts of Life (abridged version).</b><br/><br/><b>Fact #1: Rainbow Mac still has some serious growing up to do.</b><br/><br/>She's doing better but needs to realiz</span>
  <span id="freeText5847993867159585632" style="display:none"><b>First reread with my girl <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31718503-tanya" rel="nofollow noopener">Tanya</a>, January 2015.<br><br>Original rating: 4<br>New rating: 3.5</b><br><br><b>You know how this is going to go right?</b> My first review for this book was written just two months ago so don't you expect me to write another one so soon. <b>Hey, I have a life outside of GR you know (well, more or less)</b>. All you'll be getting from me is another episode in the <b>Fever Freak's Facts of Life (abridged version).</b><br><br><b>Fact #1: Rainbow Mac still has some serious growing up to do.</b><br><br>She's doing better but needs to realize moral fiber is seriously overrated.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492489332i/22521511.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Fact #2: JZB</b><br><br>Any questions? Didn't think so. Let's move on.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421429495ra/13375114.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Fact #3: Silent conversations</b><br><br>Save your saliva. It might come in handy later on (did I hear someone mention book 4 – chapter 4?).<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421429871i/13375208.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Fact #4: JB – IYCGM – IYD</b><br><br>Because who wouldn't want direct access to Jericho Freaking Barrons 24/7?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421433325i/13375719.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Fact #5: Feck. She's here.</b><br><br>Pretty much self-explanatory huh? I thought so.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421433449ra/13375745.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Fact #6: KMM needs to go on a word diet.</b><br><br>Haven't learned your lesson yet have you? Woman you <b>really</b> need to cut some of the blah blah blah crap, it just cost your book's rating half a star.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420873755i/13283338.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I rest my case. Until next time.</b><br><br>***********<br><b>Original review (November 2014)</b><br><br><b>Freaky <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-a-re-read" rel="nofollow noopener">MacHalo</a> buddy read starting November, 10 2014.</b><br><br><b>OH. WOW. Where do I start?</b> This is SO much better than the first book. Actually I could easily downgrade Darkfever to a 2.5 rating after reading Bloodfever. But I'm not *that* bad so I'll just leave my rating as it is:)<br><br><b>So that's basically me while reading the book:</b> "Bloody hell! Holy crap! You have to be kidding me! Well hello again you death-by-sex Fae, mind if I take my bra off? What the f**ck just happened?! Go girl, you show him! Arrrrggggh! Oh, swooning a bit right there! Well that was unexpected! <b>Barrons, you aggravating, infuriating, exasperating, sneaky bastard!</b> Oh no you don't! No more pink bullshit, yay! Hey Barrons, if you really want to tattoo someone I'm right here *waves frantically at Kindle screen*! <b>Oooooh that was pretty disgusting, I love it!</b> Ha ha ha ha ha! Oh wow. Freaking wow! Hallelujah! Yes yes yes!"<br><br><b>You get my drift.</b> Yes, Bloodfever was a pretty awesome read. A fast-paced, intense, emotional, exciting as hell roller-coaster ride. What impressed me most here was Moning's writing. It was alright in Darkfever but she really has outdone herself here. Moning has a <b>strange yet brilliant</b> way of giving the reader glimpses of events that have just happened behind the scenes that leaves you thinking: <b>"Wait, did I just skip a page or something?"</b> The details seem to appear magically a few paragraphs or pages later, blending effortlessly into the story. It's hard to explain really but it's one <b>fantastic writing trick</b>. That a story told in such a way would be understandable at all is amazing. Well, to be honest, I was <b>a bit clueless</b> most of the time but that's only because Moning loves to tease her readers to death, planting more questions in their little heads than she's giving them answers for. Brilliant writing I tell you! <br><br><b>Talking about the plot is nearly impossible here.</b> Too many things happening, too many twists and revelations, too much information. It's just one (choose all that apply) jaw-dropping/amazing/emotional/funny/crazy/infuriating/fascinating scene after another. <b>Want to know my favourite ones? Of course you do!</b> Here goes: Mac &amp; V'Lane at BBB (their conversation is funny as hell and what can I say? I can't resist the guy.), <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Fiona being a total bitch: this series really needed a bitch from hell ! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, Mac's dad visiting, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Dani telling Mac that there are no male sidhe-seers <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, <b>silent conversations</b> (love 'em!), the auction scene, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Mac finding out that Barrons was her sister's landlord <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, Mac's <b>involuntary beach holiday</b> and her return to a very pissed off Barrons (that'll teach him!), the <b>tattoo scene</b> (hello! Still volunteering here Barrons!), the freaking <b>Burren</b> scene from beginning to end… and its aftermath! Okay okay you win, I'll stop right there. <br><br><b>I have to say that one aspect of the plot disappointed me.</b> It's hard to talk about it without revealing anything so I guess it's spoiler time. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Grim reaper=Mallucé=culprit. That felt like a <b>cheap trick</b> to me. I expected something bigger and darker to be revealed and the fact that it was "only" Mallucé felt like a let-down. I was <b>never really impressed</b> by Mallucé. As far as bad guys go he's a bit <b>on the light side</b> and the supposed vampire act never added anything to the plot. Don't get me wrong, I love the scenes in the Burren. They are amazing and probably the best scenes in the series so far. Still, the fact that Mallucé was the bad guy felt a bit <b>anticlimactic</b> to me. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Oh wait, I just thought of something else that was a bit disappointing. Sorry, spoiler time again! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I think it's a shame that Mac didn't <b>stay part-Fae</b>, it would have been such a fantastic twist to the story! Too bad Moning didn't go with it. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Now let's talk about Rainbow Girl for a second here.</b> Mac, Mac, Mac. We weren't on the best of terms at first. How was I supposed to believe that a superficial, Barbie-looking, silly girl would turn into one of the most awesome butt kicking heroines out there? <b>I can't say she is a total badass yet but we're slowly getting there.</b> She's grown a lot since the first instalment and she's lost most of her air-headed attitude which is a huge relief. I still think that Moning <b>overdid it with the Pinky Rainbows act</b> in Bloodfever. I have no problem with a naïve, inexperienced heroine but there was no need to re-hash it all the way she did by adding layer upon layer of <b>superficial silliness</b>. Mac certainly seems to be <b>getting her act together</b> towards the end of the book and she finally holds her own against <b>Barrons and the rest of the clique.</b><br><br><b>So. Mr Barrons. Here we are.</b> After reading the first instalment I obviously thought you were an <b>aggravating bastard.</b> Because, you know, you are one. Anyway, my freaky BR friends had warned me that I would fall under your <b>exasperating-yet-irresistible spell</b> by the end of book 2. Although I have not yet fallen entirely victim to your "I'm hot, sexy and infuriating" act I have to admit I liked the <b>swoon-worthy potential</b> I had a glimpse of here <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[tattoo scene + lusty Burren = yum <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It seems some readers want romance to blossom between Mac &amp; Barrons. <b>You know what? Romance is terribly overrated.</b> Just give me the lust and I'll be the happiest of girls! As to what Barrons may or may not be: <b>I don't really have a clue</b> here except that silly little me had the very fine idea to read the Burned blurb the other day. <b>Now I know one of Barrons' dirty little secrets.</b> Clever. Very very clever of me… <br><br><b>All in all this was a pretty awesome read. What made it even more fantastic? My <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-a-re-read%20" rel="nofollow noopener"><b>MacHalo gang</b></a> of course! You guys rock.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5847993867159585632" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_817071794" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/817071794" />
    <a title="Shurrn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn"><img alt="Shurrn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410564134p2/22115857.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/817071794?book_show_action=true">Jan 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shurrn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shurrn" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback " href="/book/show/2705590-bloodfever">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=genre-scifi-and-fantasy">genre-scifi-and-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=i-spells-magic-curses">i-spells-magic-curses</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=series-unfinished">series-unfinished</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=z-own-paperback">z-own-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=genre-humor">genre-humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=i-other-dimensions">i-other-dimensions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-bad-boys">c-bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-playing-detective">c-playing-detective</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=genre-crime-or-mystery">genre-crime-or-mystery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer817071794" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8936794839391221404"><b>Things are heating up for the Fever series!</b><br/>No sophomore slump here!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420246710ra/13197115.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>It's a strange new world out there and the rules have changed: It's every princess for herself.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Ive discovered why I've been sucked into this series. <u>I can't predict or classify the characters.</u> In a world where literary characters are painfully formulaic, Karen Marie Moning is blazing her own wild road with this series and I'm just happy to be taken along for the ride.<br/><br/>I read this entire book cover-to-cover in a singl</span>
  <span id="freeText8936794839391221404" style="display:none"><b>Things are heating up for the Fever series!</b><br>No sophomore slump here!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420246710ra/13197115.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>It's a strange new world out there and the rules have changed: It's every princess for herself.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Ive discovered why I've been sucked into this series. <u>I can't predict or classify the characters.</u> In a world where literary characters are painfully formulaic, Karen Marie Moning is blazing her own wild road with this series and I'm just happy to be taken along for the ride.<br><br>I read this entire book cover-to-cover in a single day... I STILL have questions. I'm making predictions about characters and wondering about outcomes... The reader can never really be sure who is a "good guy" and who is a "bad guy" in this urban fantasy adventure on the dark streets of Dublin.<br><br>I'm beginning to think that no character is exclusively "good" or "bad" - I'm starting to believe that everyone's motives exist in a shade of grey.<br><br><b>MAC</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420242587i/13195961._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I would wear pink because I knew my future was anything but rosy. I would accessorize myself to the hilt, and I would wear flirty shoes because my world needed more beauty to counter all the ugliness in it. I would wear pink because I hated gray, I didn’t deserve white, and I was sick of black.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Mac is beginning to undergo a through mental and physical transformation. On the physical side, she's turned into black-ops Barbie by her handler.<br><br>It seems everyone wants Mac on their side, but she's learning her lesson about attracting attention... She's learning that she can't trust anybody, but she must attempt to gain information from any source possible. She's developing a set of wonderfully lethal skills and a hard shell. <br><br><b>BARRONS</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420246710i/13197116._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Barrons has something the rest of us don't have. I don't know what it is, but I feel it all the time, especially when we're standing close. Beneath the expensive clothes, unplaceable accent, and cultured veneer, there's something that never crawled all the way out of the swamp. It didn't want to. It likes it there.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> I have my predictions about <i>who</i> and <i>what</i> I think Barrons is, but I won't post them here because I don't want any of you lovely readers to confirm or deny my suspicions. I'd like for the reveal of Barrons to play out naturally as the author intended.<br><br>Barrons remains secrative, dark, and absurdly sexy... But he's damn fascinating! I'm way more interested in unraveling the mystery of Jericho Barrons than I am about anything else in this series...<br><br><b>That's saying an awful lot, because this book ramped up everything:</b><br><i>More interesting secondary-characters<br>More weird monsters roaming the streets<br>More Action and suspense<br>More blood and gore<br>More sexytimes...</i><br><br><b>But get this:<br>NOBODY HAS HAD SEX IN THIS SERIES YET!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420243250ra/13196145.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't call it Erotica...<br>I can't call it a romance...<br>This is simply one of a kind...<br><br>Unfortunately, I'll have to pause for a bit before reading the rest of the series. I received paperbacks of the first two books in this seres from my friend Terry as a Christmas gift, and now I must set out to buy the rest of the Fever Series!<br><br><b>
  <u>My other reviews in the Fever series:</u>
</b><br>1 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112750.Darkfever__Fever___1_" title="Darkfever (Fever, #1) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Darkfever</a> - Read my Review <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/817070471" rel="nofollow noopener">Here</a>.<br>2 - Read my Review <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/817071952" rel="nofollow noopener">Here</a>.<br>4 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6050298.Dreamfever__Fever___4_" title="Dreamfever (Fever, #4) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Dreamfever</a> - <div id="review_741098491" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/741098491" />
    <a title="Liz* Fashionably Late" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8191214-liz-fashionably-late"><img alt="Liz* Fashionably Late" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1385594860p2/8191214.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/741098491?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Liz* Fashionably Late" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Liz* Fashionably Late" href="/user/show/8191214-liz-fashionably-late">Liz* Fashionably Late</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191214-liz-fashionably-late?shelf=amazing-heroines">amazing-heroines</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191214-liz-fashionably-late?shelf=author-we-should-be-friends">author-we-should-be-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191214-liz-fashionably-late?shelf=awesomefest">awesomefest</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer741098491" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12624956043246397611"><b>Second Re-read:</b> November 2015.<br/>It dragged a little in the middle but the CAVE SCENE IS PERFECTION.<br/><br/><b>First Re-read:</b> November 2014 I'm still giving it <b>4 stars</b>. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>"One day you may kiss a man you cant breathe without, and find breath is of little consequence."</b>
</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-a-re-read' rel='nofollow noopener'>Buddy Read</a>
  </i>
</b> with a bunch of weirdos. Couldn't find better people to do it.<br/> <br/><b>Mac is growing and learning. </b>Never forget she has not only lost her sister but every certainty about pretty much everything since she came to Dublin and someho</span>
  <span id="freeText12624956043246397611" style="display:none"><b>Second Re-read:</b> November 2015.<br>It dragged a little in the middle but the CAVE SCENE IS PERFECTION.<br><br><b>First Re-read:</b> November 2014 I'm still giving it <b>4 stars</b>. <br><br><i>
  <b>"One day you may kiss a man you cant breathe without, and find breath is of little consequence."</b>
</i><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-a-re-read" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddy Read</a>
  </i>
</b> with a bunch of weirdos. Couldn't find better people to do it.<br> <br><b>Mac is growing and learning. </b>Never forget she has not only lost her sister but every certainty about pretty much everything since she came to Dublin and somehow she hasn't break yet. If anything, she's getting smarter, stronger. As the smart <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31718503-tanya" rel="nofollow noopener">Tanya </a>said "she's mourning over the loss of her safe, sheltered self".<br><br><b>
  <i>"I missed her hair. I missed mine. I missed my her. I missed me."</i>
</b><br><br>But that doesn't mean she won't fight. Barrons himself said when he thought she was all useless fluff and nails, she showed some teeth. <br><br>And <b>Barrons is, in my opinion, one of the best male characters ever written in the genre.</b>. He's enigmatic, he's complex, he's nothing you've ever seen and at the same time he's simple. He's exactly what he shows you. And sometimes, he let himself go and say things like this:<br><br><b>
  <i>"This wasn't what I wanted," Barrons was saying. "This isn't what I would have chosen. You must know that. It's important that you know that." </i>
</b><br><br>There's this moment when I think they've found themselves in common ground. <b>They both have been broken and survived it. </b>I think this is the moment when he sees her. And starts losing the war against himself.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Did you break once?"<br>"Yes," he said finally. <br>"Did you kill the bastard?"<br>"With my bare hands. After I kill his wife." He waved his hand at the door of the cell. "You lead, Ms. Lane. I've got your back."</i>
</b><br><br>* CAVE SCENE. CAVE SCENE *<br><u>Cave Scene.</u><br><b>cave scene.</b><br><i>cave scene.</i><br><s>cave scene.</s><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395028703ra/8937360.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Finally, I love how Mac just does what it takes in order to survive. She said it herself. There's no black and white. <br><br><b>
  <i>"There are only shades of gray. Black and white are nothing more than lofty ideals in our minds, the standards by which we try to judge things, and map out our place in the world in relevance to them."</i>
</b><br><br>So, she'll eat whatever she has to, she'll hang up with whoever she has to and she will accept whatever the night brings because she's changed too.<br><br><br>__________________________<br>First read: October 2013<br><br><b>4 *freaking solid* stars</b><br><br><i>
  <b>It's our action that defines us. What we choose. What we resist. What we're willing to die for.</b>
</i><br>I think I could describe Bloodfever as intense, fearless, brilliant, addictive, unputdownable and even then you wouldn't know how awesome this book is. <br><br><b>The writing</b> is addictive. Karen Marie Moning is a genius. <b>The plot </b>is there, I know it is, there must be... but here's the crazy thing: I have no fucking idea what the hell is going on and I don't feel betrayed at all, actually I'm so into this. I mean, she managed to capture my attention from chapter one and I just couldn't stop reading it. The best part? I'm satisfied. No complains about the lack of answers at all. <b>The characters </b>are incredibly complex and their development is amazing. Mac, once spoiled and annoying, is a total badass, funny, witty, flawed, resolved and so realistic I had to check twice if this was indeed UF material. Barrons is everything <s>I want</s> you'd ever wanted in a man if you liked incredibly strong, frustratingly enigmatic, impossible and dominating men. God, I do have issues... <br><br>And this:<br><br><b>
  <i>"Yes, I have loved, Ms. Lane, and although it‘s none of your business, I have lost. Many things. And no, I am not like any other player in this game and I will never be like V‘lane, and I get a hard-on a great deal more often than occasionally." He leaned fully against me and I gasped. <br>"Sometimes it‘s over a spoiled little girl, not a woman at all.” </i>
</b><br><br>Yes, the emotional and intense Jericho moment when you just know there's no hope for you. I'm fascinated by Fever. <br><br><b>
  <i>“The wisest man is the silent one. Examine his actions. Judge him by them.” </i>
</b><br><br>Oh, I'm judging you, Barrons... and I have some crazy theories about what you are, you sexy bastard.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382334507ra/5827206.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12624956043246397611" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer773688621" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17923651037440230824"><b>4 What-the-BLOODY-Hell Stars<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/639787.gif' width='400' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>"It’s our actions that define us.
